Tree of Presents
ϟ Values are subject to change.
When in doubt, create a price check or fair trade board on the NCC.

℗ Price check board needed.

NT Not tradeable.

buyable Currently available in the Mall.

~ This symbol means approximately. Values are subjective and items may trade higher or lower than listed.

+ This symbol means that the item trades at and above the value listed.

- This symbol denotes a range the item trades within.

Values Explained

Values are measured in Gift Box Capsules (GBCs). 1 GBC costs 200 NC. Anything up to 250 NC in value is considered ~1. All above are calculated using the standard 200 NC. Eg. ~4-5 equates to the value of 800-1000 NC.
